    The abandoned spaceport customs office creates a compelling atmosphere of isolation and liminality that effectively mirrors the character's emotional state. The contrast between cold technology and warm baking traditions works well. Sensory details like creaking security gates, dust-coated terminals, and frigid drafts successfully establish a desolate mood that enhances the character's journey toward redemption.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.3)

The world-building is the story's strongest aspect, creating a cohesive and immersive environment that enhances the supernatural elements.
